Hello folks. Actually, there could be more that is going on here, from an animal behaviour perspective. I had an Akita. 125 pounds. Drop dead handsome, built like a tank and smart as can be. My girlfriend would come up to me, just like we saw above, and love hug me. Samson, our Inu, would come up behind her, rise on his hind legs and lay his huge paws on her shoulders and apply some weight. I would be lying on the long couch, all stretched out. My GF would enter the  room and come lay on top of me, you know, to embrace and get things stirring. Samson would enter the room and stick his snout and big bear head between her body and mine. One my kids friend would come, many came over, and they would play their card games. I would get the snacks out. Nine years old lil Alex was sitting in the wingback chair with a bowl of Frito Lay chips. Samson went to sit right in front of him and waited. I was not ever in the habit to feed him that really tasty junk food. Not receiving any chips, he extended his right front leg and jabbed Lil Alex's in the thorax. The kids went "Whoa, did you see that" All of the above was sort of cute but it really was not. Samson had been castrated at eight months and by then was sixteen months old.
